 The fast of Karva Chauth is observed in the Krishna Paksha of Kartik month
 karvaa chouth striyon kaa sarvaadhik lokapriy vrath he
 Fortunate women fast on the day of Karva Chauth for Atal Suhag, husband's long life, health and good luck
 'vaaman puraana' main karvaa chouth vrath kaa varnan aata he
 Women observing Karva Chauth fast should do this fast after taking bath in the morning after taking a pledge to wish husband, son and grandson and good luck
 karvaa chouth ke vrath main shiv, parvati, kartikeya, ganesh tathaa chandramaa kaa pujan karne kaa vidhaan he
 Women take water after eating moon and pay obeisance to the moon
 puja ke baad tambe yaa mitti ke karave main chaaval, urad kii daal, suhaag kii saamagree jaise- kanghee, sheesha, sindur, chudiyaan, riban va rupaya rakhkar daan karnaa chahie tathaa saas ke paanv chhukar fal, mewa va suhaag kii sari saamagree unhen deni chahie
 The glory of Karva Chauth is an important festival of Hindus
 yah bharat ke punjab, uttar pradesh, madhya pradesh, or rajasthan kaa parv he
 It is celebrated on the Chaturthi of Krishna Paksha of Kartik month
 yah parv suhaagin striyaan manaati hai
 This fast starts after about four o'clock in the morning before sunrise and is complete after seeing the moon at night
 kaise manaaya jaataa he karvaa chouth
 
 
 On the day of Karva Chauth, married women keep a fast all day without consuming food and water
 subah suraj nikalne se pehle puja or shringaar kiye jate hai or phir sargi khai jaati he
 Sargi is the food ingredient found by mother-in-law
 shaam kii puja ke liye mahilaayein khaastaur par taiyaar hoti hai
 There is a new enthusiasm in them about grooming
 is maukey ke liye mahilaayein special mehandi bhi lagavati hai, to bindi or sindur ke liye bhi ve khaas shopping karti hai
 All women, from rural women to modern women, observe the fast of Karvachauth with great reverence and enthusiasm
 shastron ke anusaar yah vrath karthik maas ke krishnapaksh kii chandroday vyapini chaturthi ke din karnaa chahie
 Bhalchandra Ganesh ji is offered on this day to attain the longevity of the husband and good luck
 karwachouth main bhi sankashtiganesh chaturthi kii tarah din bhar upwas rakhkar raat main chandramaa ko arghya dene ke uparaant hi bhojan karne kaa vidhaan he
 In present times, most women celebrate Karvachauth Vratotsav according to the custom prevalent in their family, in which most of the women remain unharmed and wait for the moonrise
 shastron-puraanon main karvaa chouth kaa zikrakarva chouth kaa vrath saalon se chalaa aa rahaa he
 As it is mentioned in the scriptures-puranas, this fast was done with the wish of healthy and longevity of his life partner
 parv kaa swarup thode pherbadal ke saath ab bhi vahi he
 But these are not limited to husband and wife
 donon chunki gruhasthi rupi gaadi ke do pahiye he
 And are connected to the axis of allegiance
 isliye unke sambandhon par zyada dhyaan diya jaataa he
 Actually it is for the benefit and welfare of the whole family
 karvaa chouth vrath vidhaan:1
 Kartik is the law of fasting karva-chauth on the Chaturthi of Krishna Paksha
 is vrath kii visheshta yah he ki keval saubhagyawati striyon ko hi yah vrath karne kaa adhikaar he
 a woman should be of any age, caste, varna, sect, everyone has the right to observe this fast
 suhaagin stri apane pati kii aayu, swasthya or saubhaahgya kii kaamana ke liye yah vrath rakhti hai
 2
 manyata ke anusaar yah vrath baarah se solah saal tak lagaataar har saal kiya jaataa saktaa he
 This fast is practiced after the completion of the period
 haa yah bhi jaan len ki jo suhaagin striyaan is vrath ko aaajeevan rakhana chahen ve jeevanabhar is vrath ko kar sakati hai
 There is no other fortunate fast like this fast
 3
 Chandrodaya Vyapini Chaturthi of Kartik Krishna Paksha, that is, on the night of the Chaturthi in which the moon is about to be seen, take a bath in the morning on that day, taking the resolution of the age, health, good fortune of your sweetheart and remain healthy throughout the day
 4
 Worship Lord shiva-parvati, Swami Kartikeya, Ganesh and Moon on Karva Chauth
 pujan karne ke liye baaluu athwa safed mitti kii vedi banaakar in sabhi devon ko sthapit karen
 5
 shuddh ghi main aate ko senkkar usamen shakkar athwa khand milakar laddu naivedhy banaaen
 6
 vaise to bazaar main har cheez maujuud he lekin ho sake to kaali mitti main shakkar kii chaasani milakar, us mitti se taiyaar kiye gaye mitti ke karave athwa tambe ke bane hue karave istemaal karen to bahut acha rahegaa
 Karva Chauth Pujan Method: 1
 baaluu athwa safed mitti kii vedi par shiv-parvati, swami kartikeya, ganesh evam chandramaa kii sthapana karen
 After this, worship these gods
 2
 Offer naivedya by placing laddus in the pan
 ek lotaa, ek vastra or ek vishesh karvaa dakshina ke rup main arpit kar pujan samaapan karen
 Read or listen to the story of Karva Chauth fast
 3
 After the moon rises in the evening, worship the moon and offer arghya
 iske pashchaat brahman, suhaagin striyon or pati ke mata-pita ko bhojan karaaen
 Offer Dakshina to Brahmins after meals
 4
 Seek blessings by offering a lotus, clothes and special offerings to Sasuji
 yadi ve jivit na hon to unke tulya kisi anya stri ko bhent karen
 After this, you and other family members have food
 karvaa chouth main prayukt hone vaali saamagree:1
 After taking bath in the morning on the fast, start this Karva Chauth fast by speaking this resolution
 2
 Stay waterless throughout the day
 3
 Make Eight Puris of Eight Puris
 halva banaaen
 4
 pili mitti se gauri banaaen or unki god main ganeshji banaakar bithaaen
 Cover the cowpea with chunari
 bindi aadi suhaag saamagree se gauri kaa shringaar karen
 5
 jal se bharaa hua lotaa rakhen
 6
 karvaa main gehun or dhakkan main shakkar kaa bura bhar den
 Place Dakshina on it
 7
 Make a swastika on rovi karva
 8
 Worship gauri-ganesh as per tradition
 pati kii dderghaayu kii kaamana karen
 9
 karvaa par teraa bindi rakhen or gehun yaa chaaval ke teraa dane haath main lekar karvaa chouth kii katha kahen yaa sunen
 10
 katha sunne ke baad karvaa par haath ghumaakar apni saasuu ji ke pair chhukar aashirwad len or karvaa unhen de den
 11
 raatri main chandramaa nikalne ke baad chalni kii oot se use dekhen or chandramaa ko ardhya den
 After this, take blessings from your husband
 unhen bhojan karaaen or swayan bhi bhojan kar len
 12
 saas apni bahu ko sargi bhejti he
 Sargi contains sweets, fruits, sevaiyan etc
 iskaa seven mahilaayein karwachouth ke din surya nikalne se pehle karti hai
 13
